<Rate>5<//Rate><text>Lived in the immediate areas my entire life and always assumed this place was only a bar. Well now I live basically across the street and I had to go check out this bay famous garlic fried chicken I've been hearing about.

We decided to go with the small bucket of garlic fried chicken that comes with 8 potato wedges which are 2 large potatoes that have been qartered. We couldn't be more pleased with what we received. The flavors of the wedges are great and last. Not like other chicken chains where it seems like you're eating straight potatoes. The chicken was heavily seasoned with garlic but surprisingly it's not overpowering at all. The garlic goes with the fried flavor perfectly. The chicken was moist and juicy and very meaty. I will be back with out a doubt . It's a very home-style joint that serves up some great comfort food and with relatively good prices.  The small bucket with 8 wedges was 16 bucks and the regular chicken is 15 I believe .<//text><pics>None</pics><Response>None<//Response><gmap_id>0x808576ad818f1615:0x53a10e2939595dac< /gmap_id></record>

<time>1603831786581<//time>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
<text>Many of the recycling centers in Temecula have closed and I searched to find a replacement. SA is a great place to take your cans and plastic bottles.
It can be a bit intimidating but not to worry, just go to the second entrance marked for cans and bottles and pull INDOORS. Yes it out of the sun and in  a large warehouse type of building. Park your car and get a cart and some empty plastic barrels and load up your cans,plastic etc . Wheel them over to the weight station and very friendly and helpful staff weigh your recycling. Then you get a receipt and go to the corner office a get your cash. In my opinion, the rate of pay was very fair. Highly recommend!
They also do a lot more than just cans and bottles, check out their web site for all the materials that they recycle.
Went back for another visit and was pleased with the great service. I was amazed that there was as many women as men recycling. I guess every one can use an extra buck. Every one had masks so I felt safe. The only thing that I found to be a new rule was all caps had to be removed from the plastic bottles, I had to get out of line and spend 10 minutes removing bottle caps. Also the times for returns of CRV materials is 8 am to 1 PM Monday - Sat. They call this place rock bar and I gotta say, this place does rock! GOOD PEEPS! From the cool locals, with their tight shirts and hair-cuts, to the cultured bartendress who recommended the PERFECT mezcal that brought my fianc√© and I back to our time spent lounging on the small private islands off the Mexican coast.The pool table was lively and crowded but our little pupper didn't seem to mind. This place is a dog bar, but beware, some are not so nice, ME-OW.

Our only concern when coming to this far flung end of 'el mision' was the gang of unsavory gentlemen crowded outside the bicycle store next door. STRANGER DANGER!

All in all, the atmosphere was 'rocky' but pleasant, a perfect dive bar to head to after a long night of pre-paddy's day bar hopping and debauchery.

EDIT: Had to take a star off, my wonderful fianc√© left her Lora Pianino pashmina and when we got it back there was a massive dark stain. I'm really disapointed in you, rock bar.</Review>

Jess Killips< /user_name>
< time>
1378276345818< /time>
< Rating>
4< /Rating>
< review>
Powerful, tasty cocktails. Having tried most all of their menu, their most artfully crafted cocktail is the blood and sand which I would return for in a heartbeat. The others were not made to the caliber I am used to at Bourbon and Branch, my gold standard for cocktail making. I love the vibe, ample seating, and friendly bartenders. I heard you can order bites, and they will deliver from Front Porch across the street.

A few of the drinks I tried...

*Gold Digger ($11) - 3.5 STARS: London Gin, Pear Liqueur, Champagne, ginger, peach. Reminds me of a Mike's Hard Lemonade. Very tasty, a bit sweet. Refreshing.

* Real Thunderberg ($9) - 1 STAR: Four Roses, Bunderberg Ginger, Underberg. Tastes like medicine.

* Rhuby Mule ($10?) - 3 STARS: Vodka, Cherry Heering, ginger ale, rhubarb bitters. Love moscow mules but this cherry version was way too sweet for me.

* Soft Rock ($10?) - 3.5 STARS: Lillet Blanc, soda, lemon, cucmber. Refreshing and tasty.

* ICHI Rock ($10) - 3.5 STARS: London Gin, St. Germain, Yuzu, grapefruit bitters. This was another one that reminded me of Mike's Hard Lemonade. Super refreshing and tasty but not the type of cocktail I gravitate towards. Too frou frou for me.

They also have a decent list of special cocktails listed on their board, which includes my favorite - Blood and Sand.

Tip: Cash Only.< /review>

< Review>
Dr. Shiflett has been my kids' dentist for the past 9 years, since they were 1 and 2.... I couldn't have picked a better dentist for them.... The Dr. Is patient and kind with the kids. She talks them through every step using kid friendly language to keep them comfortable and at ease. They also look forward to their care pack that includes a new toothbrush, toothpaste and floss.

As a parent, I'm happy and comfortable to see my kids happy and comfortable with Dr. Shiflett and her staff. The staff are super sweet and friendly with the kids and the parents. Another plus is that as a parent you can be in the same room with your child as they're getting treated.

< Review>
My wife and I LOVE this dental office. We were recommended here by my coworker and I couldn't be happier with the recommendation.

Every single dentist office I have ever been to, there has been a certain degree of selling or cross selling involved with their approach. One dentist would recommend a cavity fill, another would oversell and recommend a root canal. I have experienced this throughout my life. However, my very first appointment at Dr. Shiflett's office was completely different. Dr. Shiflett shows a level of compassion and dedication to her clientele that I generally do not see in other dentists. Our very first visit to her office was to check on some areas of concern for our son. After a thorough cleaning, Dr. Shiflet took a look at the cavity and recommended that we continue to brush and keep an eye on the cavity. My wife and I went in there fully expecting to have a full on procedure done that day!

Of all the times we have been there, everyone we have ever dealt with has been absolutely wonderful. They are all very caring and very good with our son, who can be very fussy especially when it comes to the dentist's office. The facility it self is very clean, welcoming, and whimsically decorated to cater to children and has toys and a movie playing in the waiting room. We will most likely be taking our son here for as long as possible.<//Review>

There is one problem, can't ignore it, costs a star at least. On a busy night, it's too LOUD. Unfortunately, all the surfaces are hard and it's a small space, so sound gets reflected back easily. <username>Brian Auerbach<//username><Date>1550380910259< /Date>< rating>

< review>
We were a table of 6 seated in the back, near the kitchen, which was almost definitely the quietest place. It was still fairly loud and somewhat difficult to hear the people at our table.

As far as the food, we were mostly very happy. The dates, mushroom dish, turkey meatballs (two orders of these, one perfect, one overcooked), skirt steak, squash dish, and the queso bites (these were excellent with both the chorizo and ham) were all at least above average. I would say no particular dish stood out that I'd need to come back for, but the overall meal was very good.

The service was really good - our server was very attentive, and the runners kept our waters topped up consistently. Most of the drinks were enjoyed by all, though they varied a bit in strength (some just right and some a bit heavy-handed - that's the best way to make a mistake).

Ambiance: 3
Food: 4
Service: 4+

This is a good tapas restaurant, and the only of its kind in the area. I enjoyed it and will be back when I'm in the mood for that type of dining.< /review>

< review>
Too bad there's not an option for a negative rating.  What a horrible experience.  The environment is all open concept and hard surfaces so the noise level is stunningly loud.  While seated promptly for our reservation, it took several minutes for our server to arrive.  Our drink order took at least 15 minutes to be delivered, which was a consistent problem throughout the evening.  We are martini drinkers, so to be served martinis in a 3 oz. 1920's era champagne glass was not impressive.  The food options are assorted, but the meal was not good.  The lamb chops were undercooked, the skirt steak stringy, and the shrimp and garlic with bread inedible.  The sodium content of the shrimp made it impossible to eat, and the bread was a delivery system for butter, and was also salted.  And this is not a restaurant run by people new to the game.   This family runs multiple stores in the South Bay, this being their latest.   The service was poor, and the Owner made it a point to tell us to remember his face, as he was the Owner, to which one of our party replied that he should remember his face, as he is the client.  Arrogant and out of touch.   We hated the experience and will not return.</review>

After reading the Eater article on Gabi James I rushed to make a reservation! The decor is really nice and the menu looked promising. However, our service was less than stellar. My mother's wine was forgotten, we asked for a third set of silverware multiple times, the fish was "boneless" but had many many bones, and probably the biggest kicker was a flub on my allergen request. The server was unaware of what was and was not gluten free on the menu until after serving it to us (even though I made it aware before ordering). This rating truly comes down to service and not the food. We had a discussion with the manager, but all that was offered was a few meager sorries no action. Won't be returning to what might have been a great local spot.< /Review>

< review>
My husband and I were excited to try this place and we were not disappointed. The restaurant is stunning inside and everyone there from the waiters to the bartenders to the owners were friendly and helpful. They seemed genuinely happy to be there and enthusiastic about the menu.  Sara and Adam (the owners) were both there and made a point to check in with us.

The cocktails are amazing and unique and they have a comprehensive gin list for those gin lovers. We had the ‚Äújalape√±o your business‚Äù and the ‚Äúsloe your roll‚Äù and loved them. My husband noticed they also had a really great selection of beers that are hard to find anywhere else.

For dinner we had the croquettes (delicious), tortilla (better than I‚Äôve had anywhere - even in Spain), the citrus salad, one of the pastas with clams and jamon, and the oxtail ragu. Everything was amazing and modern and the oxtail is a real standout - so so good. For dessert we had the churros which I loved because they weren‚Äôt overpoweringly sweet.  We also split another dessert that was somewhere between a flan and a creme br√ªl√©e - to die for. It would be worth it just to stop in for a glass of wine and dessert if you‚Äôre in the mood for something sweet.

Overall we were really happy with everything and look forward to coming back!< /review>

The only thing that sucks about that is the online sign-up assigns a unit for you randomly without a personal visual of the unit first. Luckily my unit was computer selected away from the front gate but I could see how if I got a unit right in front I may have disliked it. There is a downside to this place which is not nearly as prominent as it is at the storage place across the street though. My gripe is about the few obvious transient customers that store the only junk they own in a unit here. I was harrassed and almost forced to physically defend myself against a drunk guy while entering the facility not too long ago (you can guess what he looked like...dark)! I remember fondly when they first set up shop two~three years ago, setting up their tables in front of Whole Foods parking lot.  Nowadays, they are the neighborhood staple, commanding long lines for their delicious morsels.  Highly recommend this place and get your fill on some amazing tacos!< /Review>
